  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_8a85e9bd-5db6-452f-b332-976613e8e8ee'
      });

  <span id="freeText16314356446376619105" style="display:none">If the world you lived in was someday revealed to be nothing but a lie, would you really want the truth? Elizabeth McBeth did, and she's paid the price for it...<br /><br />After almost 10 years since Liz's mother was taken from her, Liz finally found her mother, Mary. But Mary has been forever changed, something that Liz will have to accept. The beginning of happier times, one would think...<br /><br />The conspiracy has been exposed; Liz, Vincent, Mary and Michael had all thought that the vampire plot had been destroyed. They should have never underestimated Klein. <br /><br />Klein has reinforced his armies, splitting the entire vampire species with the question... is Klein the vampiric messiah? Unfortunately for the heroes and the world itself, Klein has set in motion a plan that will destroy the world and recreate it in his own image.<br /><br />Will the group be able to defeat Klein and restore the balance to nature? Or are they already doomed?</span>

<span id="freeTextContainer17014038556204412741">Revenge served?<br/>This book was better then the first. You get to see who the real Vincent is and we already know Michael. What we don't know is who Lizzy will pick to be her mate. When you read who she chooses your mind will be blown, I know mine was. The twists that happen in this book and evolutions are great! Not to mention they all now face a much more intents threat then what they could ever imagine!! <br/></span>

          </span>

    <a title="Kelli Smith" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/16743439-kelli-smith"><img alt="Kelli Smith" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388449664p2/16743439.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelli Smith" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelli Smith" href="/user/show/16743439-kelli-smith">Kelli Smith</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/16743439-kelli-smith?shelf=ol-s-shelf">ol-s-shelf</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer705699408" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12037029948555881981">OL Ramos's second book in The Keeper series is exuberant. The saga continues with Liz, Michael, and Vincent and their goal to preserve the Supernatural Veil from the human world. This book may not contain quite as much action as the first, but it delves into the personal background of Michael and Vincent. The struggle for Liz to choose between the two is starting to unravel and a winner will emerge.<br/>More of the battle continues with Klein from Book one revealing more the Supers and their prominen</span>
  <span id="freeText12037029948555881981" style="display:none">OL Ramos's second book in The Keeper series is exuberant. The saga continues with Liz, Michael, and Vincent and their goal to preserve the Supernatural Veil from the human world. This book may not contain quite as much action as the first, but it delves into the personal background of Michael and Vincent. The struggle for Liz to choose between the two is starting to unravel and a winner will emerge.<br />More of the battle continues with Klein from Book one revealing more the Supers and their prominence in this book. The last half of the book has really great action scenes, and details the chaos that the three will soon be up against.<br /><br />OL Ramos is an exquisite writer and has an imagination that is unparallel. His characters are growing and maturing and devulging more pieces of themselves and their history that is truly making this a great series. All the while, new characters are being brought in at a nice easy pace so as not to overwhelm the reader.<br /><br />If you have not read the first book The Awakening:Keeper, I highly recommend getting it. You will be back for this one soon after.<br /><br />Bravo OL Ramos ! </span>
  <a data-text-id="12037029948555881981" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/29621401-elle-bee-double-u?shelf=paranormal">paranormal</a>,

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer3429603003" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16902826220747680233">Revenge picks up a couple months after the trio of Liz, Michael, and Vincenzo have confronted and taken on The Coronam. <br/>Liz has finally found "validation" when she found her mother with Klein. But the problems for everyone is just starting. Liz still must learn more about herself and her keeper nature, as well as sort through all the feelings she has mixed up with between Michael and Vincenzo. But that's not the worst of their problems. Klein is still out and determine to extract his revenge and</span>
  <span id="freeText16902826220747680233" style="display:none">Revenge picks up a couple months after the trio of Liz, Michael, and Vincenzo have confronted and taken on The Coronam. <br />Liz has finally found "validation" when she found her mother with Klein. But the problems for everyone is just starting. Liz still must learn more about herself and her keeper nature, as well as sort through all the feelings she has mixed up with between Michael and Vincenzo. But that's not the worst of their problems. Klein is still out and determine to extract his revenge and capture Liz. <br /><br />I will say compared to the first one, this didn't have so much action, which I really thought was funny since majority of the first one was more world building and probably didn't get into the action until about the 55% marker. The choice between Vincent and Michael while is a hard one for Liz to choose, I was a bit saddened by the choice...but alas I'm sure there is something great in store for us. The relationship with Mary and Liz was really strained which I can understand considering she's been missing for 10 years and is still the same age and has been turned. </span>

<div id="review_713514429" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/713514429" />
    <a title="Rebecca Edwards" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/20194723-rebecca-edwards"><img alt="Rebecca Edwards" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1368116964p2/20194723.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/713514429?book_show_action=true">Sep 06, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Rebecca Edwards" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Rebecca Edwards" href="/user/show/20194723-rebecca-edwards">Rebecca Edwards</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer713514429" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15697815925658590749">I loved this book. I couldn't put it down. O.L. Ramos pulled me in from the beginning of this story and kept me right there until the end. This is the second book in The Keeper Series.<br/><br/>I have to say that I love Vincent. Vincent is a vampire who's in love with Izzy a Keeper. He believes that Izzy is the reincarnation of his past love Isabella and the only one who can fill the hole inside of him. He loves to drink a lot. He's got all kinds of powers and he's funny as hell to boot at times. He doesn</span>
  <span id="freeText15697815925658590749" style="display:none">I loved this book. I couldn't put it down. O.L. Ramos pulled me in from the beginning of this story and kept me right there until the end. This is the second book in The Keeper Series.<br /><br />I have to say that I love Vincent. Vincent is a vampire who's in love with Izzy a Keeper. He believes that Izzy is the reincarnation of his past love Isabella and the only one who can fill the hole inside of him. He loves to drink a lot. He's got all kinds of powers and he's funny as hell to boot at times. He doesn't let many people get close to him except for Michael a werewolf who he's known for a long time and thinks of as family, Mary, another vampire, and Izzy, the girl he loves and his best friend loves.<br /><br />Michael is a werewolf and he's also the Alpha of the Ironskin Pack. His pack is made up of werewolf's, a couple vampires, and slayers. Michael is in love with Izzy also. One of his abilities is that he's an Empath which means he knows how Izzy feels about him and Vincent. Michael can be funny at times but he's more serious than Vincent but just as loveable as Vincent.<br /><br />Mary is a vampire and she also happens to be Izzy's mom. She was held prisoner by Klein until she managed to escape with help a year ago. She thinks that she could have a chance at happiness and love again with either Vincent or Michael. Mary knows how they both feel about Izzy and tells her she needs to make up her mind. It's been going on long enough and she won't know if she can be with one until Izzy finally decides who she wants to be with.<br /><br />Izzy's life is a constant adventure. She's always in danger as long as Klein is alive. He wants to destroy the Super's and he wants Izzy. If that isn't enough Izzy is in love with both Vincent and Michael. She loves one as a woman loves a man and the other as a brother but which one is which. This is what she needs to figure out while hoping nothing happens to anyone in her family. The last thing she wants to do is hurt anyone.<br /><br />This book has almost everything I could want in a book. There's a hint at romance that I can't wait to see blossom into full blown romance. I would love to see how the romance blossoms between them and if they all find love. This book also was full of adventure, hope, and fear. I felt like I was a part of the story and can't wait for more in this series so that I can return to this fabulous world. I will definitely be recommending this book to all of my friends. O.L. Ramos you have a new fan thanks to this fantastic read. </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer16929027979939755846">**I received a copy of this book in exchange for an honest review**<br/><br/>The second book in The Keeper series is just as good as the first one, The Keeper Awakening.You should definitely read the first book in the series though, you would most likely be lost if you read the series out of sync.<br/>So, we pick up a few months later after the ordeal at The Coronam. In this installment Liz is feeling a bit lonely and like the odd man, or should I say woman, out. She starts to get a little whiny but at least s</span>
  <span id="freeText16929027979939755846" style="display:none">**I received a copy of this book in exchange for an honest review**<br /><br />The second book in The Keeper series is just as good as the first one, The Keeper Awakening.You should definitely read the first book in the series though, you would most likely be lost if you read the series out of sync.<br />So, we pick up a few months later after the ordeal at The Coronam. In this installment Liz is feeling a bit lonely and like the odd man, or should I say woman, out. She starts to get a little whiny but at least she knows she is and it's not her character trait at all. <br />Michael, and Vincenzo are investigating and trying to gather allies for whatever revenge Klein is planning. Which they all know he is planning something and it is going to be BIG. Mary is at Angel's Retreat with Liz but she's training all of the time, so that leaves Liz all by her lonesome. So she comes up with a plan to gain a little freedom and sanity. And that's when all of the trouble starts. Seriously, this quartet finds themselves in crazy situations quite often, lol. Even though they are always on Klein's tail, it seems they can never gather enough info to be one step ahead of him and stop him. When they finally think they can thwart Klein's plan, they are thrown another obstacle their way. While and in the midst of all of the action, Liz is still trying to figure out who she wants to be with. And then we are left with a crazy a** cliffhanger. Which I will agree with the author's last words on the pages. You have to leave them wanting more. No matter how much I hate cliffhangers, I love them just as much, lol. I like being teased and wanting more, lol, yes I know how that sounds but it's the truth. In both cases lol. <br /><br />Another great read! And I cannot wait to see what kind of trouble these guys get into next, lol. <br /> <br /></span>

  <span id="freeText7525726642509849495" style="display:none">Liz should be happy. She has her mother back. After all this time, but Mary is different now that she is a Vampire. Things are different for Liz also. Vincent has to make everyone she ever knew forget her just so they will be safe. Klein is still on the loose. It seems that every time they turn around someone else is showing up trying to hurt them and they have to prove themselves as the good guys. All while they are trying to find Klein and put a stop to whatever his plans are. During all of this Liz is still going through her own personal battle. Who will she choose? Michael or Vincent? There seems to be another player in that game. Mary seems to be getting very close to one of them as well. Does Mary have strong feelings for one of them? Will that thought help Liz make up her mind?<br /><br />I absolutely LOVED this book. When I talk about things that they had to go through I think Michael had the worst. I cringed the whole time I read that part just thinking about what he was going through. I hope that little tid bit intrigues you to read the book. lol. There is always something going on, it seems like they never really get a chance to rest in this book. Or for the budding romance to evolve. I am now eager to read book 3 to see where it all goes. I definitely recommend reading but you want to read book 1 first.<br /><br />' Read and Reviewed by LSK Sweetheart Reviews '</span>

<script type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('GJIwwOrHHA8n6aG0s4fn1Q92PBU0As1OrQSgrrlixxIPNlwbqy/gAkfksr+JzLnlx6khguUN35lEoqDY5Tk9pA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('5eoBu1rk4JtSOxNehYD4L7c1Xqi/rE6dUK2e4OAfsubyTm1gGwwcljI2AFW/y6Yff+pDP26jXEq5C56WvERIUA==')})
  }
//]]>
</script>
